				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'HK', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20280621' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                            </div>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 3360;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		function ShowAllLanguages( elLink )
		{
			if ( typeof GetUsabilityTracker !== 'undefined' )
				GetUsabilityTracker().AddEvent( 1002 );

			$J('table.game_language_options tr').show();
			$J( elLink ).hide();
			return false;

							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<i>Feel the excitement of flying the Su-25T "Frogfoot" attack jet and the TF-51D "Mustang" in the free-to-play Digital Combat Simulator World! Two free maps are also included: The eastern Black Sea and the Mariana Islands.</i><br><br><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/maincol_gradient_rule.png?t=1693606790"><br><br><strong><h2 class="bb_tag">Digital Combat Simulator World</h2></strong><br><br><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/Banner-1.gif?t=1693606790"><br><br>Digital Combat Simulator World (DCS World) is a free-to-play digital battlefield game.<br>Our dream is to offer the most authentic simulation of military aircraft, ground and armor vehicles, and naval units possible. This free download includes a vast area of the Caucasus region as well as a free Mariana Islands map. It includes one of the most powerful Mission Editors ever designed, network play, and hundreds of AI weapons systems, ground units, armored vehicles, air defense systems, and ships. It also includes a free Russian Sukhoi Su-25T ground attack jet and the famous WWII North American TF-51D Mustang fighter. <br><br><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/Banner-2.gif?t=1693606790"><br><br>DCS is a true "sandbox" simulation that is also designed to cover multiple time periods of interest such as WWII, Korean War, Vietnam, Gulf War and others.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/Banner-3.gif?t=1693606790"><br><br> Current regions to battle include the Back Sea, Marianas, Nevada Test and Training Range, Persian Gulf, English Channel, Syria, and Normandy 1944. <br><br><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/Banner-4.gif?t=1693606790"><br><br>DCS World is a deep and realistic simulation that can be tailored to suit any level of experience. Our mission is to deliver excellence and make your dreams a virtual reality. We do this by offering training for complex weapons systems like the DCS: F/A-18C Hornet, DCS: F-16C Viper, DCS: AH-64D, and many more. The next step is the real thing!<h2 class="bb_tag">KEY FEATURES</h2><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/maincol_gradient_rule.png?t=1693606790"><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>A realistic Free-to-Play digital battlefield.<br></li><li>Eagle Dynamics Graphics Engine (EDGE) that looks amazing from 0 to 80,000 feet.<br></li><li>Free American TF-51 Mustang and Russian Su-25T attack jet.<br></li><li>Multi-layer volumetric cloudscapes with wind, precipitation, air pressure, and more.<br></li><li>Highly detailed map of the Caucasus region that encompass southwestern Russia and Georgia. 20 operational airbases, detailed terrain, and both civil and military infrastructure with thousands of kilometers of usable roads and railway.<br></li><li>Detailed recreation of the Mariana Islands including 1,500 x 1,000km of land and ocean for naval operations that includes Andersen AFB and the airfields on Rota, Tinian and Saipan.<br></li><li>Includes hundreds of fully operational weapons systems, ground vehicles, ships and AI-controlled aircraft.<br></li><li>The Mission Editor allows rapid mission generation and the possibility to create your own missions and campaigns for unlimited gameplay.<br></li><li>Multi-Crew enables full network play in the same aircraft in Multiplayer.<br></li><li>Thousands of online servers offering PvP and PvE.<br></li><li>Mouse interactive 6 degrees of Freedom (6DOF) cockpits<br></li><li>Accurate flight models, weapons systems, sensors, targeting systems and sounds.<br></li><li>Hundreds of missions and campaigns with new campaigns continually created.<br></li><li>Community Files section offering endless user created modifications, skins, missions and more.<br></li><li>Full virtual reality support.</li></ul><br><img src="https://cdn.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/223750/extras/Banner-5.gif?t=1693606790">						</div>

	<div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" class="review_box    partial">
		<div id="ReviewContentsummary144542430">
			
			<div class="leftcol" id="ReviewContentsummary144542430_leftcol">
				<div class="avatar">
					<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561199512389493/">

				<div class="persona_name"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561199512389493/" data-miniprofile="1552123765">󠀡󠀡</a></div>
								<div class="num_owned_games"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561199512389493/games/?tab=all">帐户内拥有 2 项产品</a></div>
												<div class="num_reviews"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561199512389493/recommended/">1 篇评测</a></div>

			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary144542430_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561199512389493/recommended/223750/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">
						<img id="votingImage" src="https://store.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_thumbsUp_v6.png" width="40" height="40">
													<img class="responsive_voting_image" src="https://community.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/public/images/apphubs/bigpicture/thumbs_upselected.png" width="40" height="40">

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是通过 Steam 序列号激活的" src="https://store.cloudflare.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_key.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 486.2 小时												（评测时 433.8 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary144542430_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：8 月 19 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 序列号													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					DCS 老牌玩家外设【萌新请私聊推荐】<br><br>1.成都造火控面板、成都造起降面板<br>2.VPC T50 CM2油门、摇杆<br>3.iPad Air4 基于Helios实现分屏触控<br>4.Stream Deck XL 基于DCS Interface实现按键扩展（包括冷启、UFC等功能）<br>5.Track IR NP5头瞄<br>6.模拟工坊铝型材支架+自制平板电脑转接支架和Stream Deck磁吸转接支架<br>7.VKB T-rudder MKIV<br><br>另外 别看 这号的模拟飞行和DCS 以及EVE Warframe才不过一百多小时 其实就是个登录器 玩的最长的是EVE 06年开始玩的吧 也陆陆续续退坑摸鱼了 13年接触了模拟飞行<br>最终还是回到了F/A18C，并不是A10C做的不好，而是感觉没有认认真真脚踏实地的飞好F/A18C，看了B站上的大神才知道自己太弱了，也许升空就是靶机吧！雷达锁定、敌我识别、数据链、空中加油、电子战、格斗等都是我的知识盲区，于是乎我果断把猪杆拆下，换上了F/A18C的替换杆，下定决心飞好18。每天进步一点点，每天都有成就感，以前以为模飞很孤单，然而暖心的是我找到了志同道合的朋友，也许这就是模飞的魅力，在吃透18C前不准备再写评测了，踏踏实实吃透模组才是合格的模飞玩家<br>2020.3.29<br>F18已经吃灰，开始研究捣鼓A10C了，不愧是完成度最高的模组，光手册就700页，有点奔溃。为了体验，我甚至上了VR，真香嘿嘿<br>2020.3.30<br>前前后后在这游戏上投入也有好几千了，基本大家推荐的模组全部购买，电脑内存加到128G，嘿嘿！总算可以玩服务器了。不知不觉就98小时了，目前基本掌握了F18的核心，从冷启动、起飞、降落、case1航降再到雷达、空对空、空对地，算是入门了。<br>2020.3.21更新<br>卡在了F/A-18C航降CASE1，卡了两天毫无脾气，同事说我疯了，每天晚上就盯着个破飞机练航降。皇天不负有心人，第34个小时，航降case1终于成功了，泪目<br><br>众所周知，DCS WORLD是一款免费游戏，目前为止已经花了2K买飞机，4W+2w买座舱及外设，3H看手册，5H学会冷启动及起飞，3H学会航电及目视进近直接进场落地，通场进近落地是真的难，目前卡在了通场，武器系统啥的还没学，这游戏估计没个正儿八经2000小时根本就算外行.我甚至还用业余时间去考了直升机执照，那么有的人问了 为啥不考民航呢，那是因为裸眼视力不够 再加上没选上被淘汰了，这可真是比失恋都难受，←这段可以忽略<br><br><b>之后的一年里我想说 </b><br><div class="bb_h1">1.理性消费</div>如果你只是对飞行类游戏有兴趣，但是又不确定自己是不是那么热爱，我个人建议你不要买DLC，DCSW平台是免费游玩的，提供Su-25T和TF-51两种免费机型可供玩家游玩，作为新玩家我建议你先把Su-25T玩好，起码最基本的起落要练会。等你会飞Su-25T以后，假如你依然对这游戏有兴趣，甚至对飞行的热爱更深了，那么你可以考虑购买自己喜欢的DLC了。这里也说一下，购买DLC要理性对待，先买一款自己兴趣最大的来学习，不要一次性买很多，相信我，你学不过来的，买了也是浪费钱。这里提一句，FC3自身包含Su-27、Su-33、F-15C、MiG-29等，买了FC3的朋友就不要另买Su-27和F-15C了，但是如果你只对美机感兴趣那只买一个F-15C就行了（反之亦然），没必要买FC3，不过我个人认为作为新人趁着打折入手一个FC3的话最划算。<br>2.保持耐心<br>因为飞行模拟本身的局限性，很多新人入坑后很难找到稳定的老手带飞（毕竟还要工作、还要照顾家里，很多老飞也因此放弃了模飞），这在无形中更是增加了飞行模拟类游戏的门槛，这么多年来，我也见过了很多新人弃坑。对于这个，我只想说——保持耐心！！买了自己喜欢的机型DLC后，一定要自己耐心的照着手册和游戏内的训练任务去学习，遇到不懂的问题可以加模飞群或者去一些模飞论坛问，知识都是积累起来的，等你积累了一定的模飞知识后你学习新机型的速度也会逐渐加快。万事开头难，只要你有耐心，保持着那份对飞行的执着与热爱，你一定可以熬过去。<br><div class="bb_h1">3.模拟飞行不等于真实飞行</div>这个没啥好啰嗦的，只是想劝大家别太钻牛角尖，有些模拟不到位的地方自己知道就行（不过说真的，ED还算是良心了，官方出的机型模拟度还可以），吐槽可以，但是却没必要去争论什么。当初我因为在《MSFS》里面经常飞Cessna 172R，所以当我第一次坐进C172R座舱的时候就感到了无比的熟悉，这个游戏可能也能为你带来快乐 所以 请不要盲目差评 如果因为自身对游戏不理解 反手一个差评 ,那么请移步 隔壁战争雷霆吧<br><div class="bb_h1">4.游戏外设很重要</div>作为模飞玩家，有一套飞行摇杆外设是很必要的，不但能增加代入感，还能使你更好的控制飞机飞行。当你对模飞的热爱程度很高的时候，你就该攒钱买一套自己的模飞设备了。<br>PS：这个可以参考我主页的下拉简介<br><br>所以 请萌新们 多加练习 多学习！致敬各位飞友 感谢！~					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>
